FNV PBR PPLIGHTING PASS RESOURCE PROVENANCE FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Resolve where BA9EE0 entry +0x0C resource-array values come from at callsites.
2. Separate true texture/resource pointers from dynamic mode/type registers before assigning PBR map semantics.
3. Keep visible PBR replacement blocked unless the resource path to E7EA00/SetTexture is concrete.
